Prior: brep-render sub-α shipped: NEW `crates/brep-render/src/lib.rs` (full rewrite from 4-line stub) with public `RenderMesh { positions: Vec<[f32; 3]>, normals: Vec<[f32; 3]>, indices: Vec<u32>, face_labels: Option<Vec<u64>> }` struct + `RenderMesh::from_buffers(positions: &[[f32; 3]], indices: &[u32], face_labels: Option<&[u64]>) -> RenderMesh` constructor — a CPU-side flat-shaded vertex-tripled mesh-conversion substrate. No GPU dep, no `gfx` dep, no `winit` dep, no editor wiring, no glam / wgpu / bytemuck. **Layering — buffer-typed input (LOAD-BEARING deviation from spec)**: `brep-render` is in the `forbidden-dep` lint's `RENDERER_CRATES` set, and PLAN.md §1.3 rule 6 forbids renderer crates from depending on game-domain crates (and `rge-cad-core` is game-domain via `rge-cad-` prefix). The substrate therefore consumes raw `&[[f32; 3]]` positions, `&[u32]` indices and an optional opaque `&[u64]` per-triangle face-label slice instead of `rge_cad_core::Tessellation` directly. A caller in `cad-projection` (or similar Tier-2 bridge crate) that owns both `Tessellation` and a `RenderMesh` consumer composes the conversion in two lines (`tess.face_labels.as_ref().map(|v| v.iter().map(|t| t.0).collect())` + `RenderMesh::from_buffers(&tess.positions, &tess.indices, labels.as_deref())`). `TopologyFaceId(pub u64)` is wire-compatible — `face_id.0` is a lossless u64 round-trip. **Shading model**: flat-shaded vertex tripling (each input triangle becomes 3 independent output vertices carrying the triangle's face normal); 3× vertex count vs. input; degenerate triangles (`|cross| < 1e-6`) emit `[0, 0, 0]` normal rather than NaN (matches cad-projection picking's `EPSILON`); face_labels preserved 1:1 in input order (NO skip / reorder / filter — desync between output triangle index and face_label would break the next sub-dispatch's selection-feedback path). Output `indices` are dense `[0, 1, 2, ..., 3n-1]`. 8 unit tests in `lib.rs::tests` (empty input → empty output; single CCW XY triangle → +Z normal; cuboid → 36 verts / 36 normals / 36 indices / 12 face_labels; PosZ face triangles all share `(0, 0, +1)` normal; face_labels preserved 1:1; unlabeled input → unlabeled output; degenerate triangle → zero normal not NaN; indices dense 0..3n) + 3 integration tests in NEW `crates/brep-render/tests/render_mesh_smoke.rs` (cuboid 6-axis face-normal verification; extrude n=4 triangle-count match per D-projection-β contract `4n - 4 = 12`; revolve partial n=4 segments=8 face_labels count round-trip per D-projection-γ contract `2*n*segments + 2*(n-2) = 68`). All CAD-shaped fixtures are duplicated inline (canonical Cuboid 8-vert layout / Extrude 8-vert two-ring layout / Revolve partial 36-vert structurally-correct layout) rather than imported from cad-core because rule 6 forbids the dep. Cargo.toml gains zero production deps (the dispatch's planned `rge-cad-core` prod dep would have tripped rule 6); workspace defaults sufficient for `#[cfg(test)]` inline + integration tests. **Failure-class declaration `//! Failure class: snapshot-recoverable` added** to `brep-render/src/lib.rs`; the corresponding `failure-class` exemption for `crates/brep-render/Cargo.toml` REMOVED from `tools/architecture-lints/exemptions.toml` (rollout-debt count 31 → 30, substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0). The first piece of the Render-backed face-selection chapter (active 2026-05-10) — fills an EMPTY-STUB on the rendering tier with a callable, tested, headless `buffer-triple → RenderMesh` primitive. **Does NOT bring up rendering**: no GPU, no window, no surface, no triangle on screen; produces the data shape the eventual gfx pass will upload. +11 net workspace tests (was 2250; now **2261 tests**); 240 → 241 binaries (+1 for render_mesh_smoke.rs); brep-render 0 → 11 tests (+11 net = 8 unit + 3 integration); cad-core unchanged at 471; cad-projection unchanged at 116. Prior: Headless face-picking sub-α shipped: NEW `crates/cad-projection/src/picking.rs` module with `Ray { origin: [f32;3], direction: [f32;3] }`, `FacePick { entity, owner, face_id, t, triangle_index }`, and `CadProjection::pick_face(&Ray, &World, &OperatorGraph) -> Option<FacePick>` — a CPU-only ray-vs-`ProjectedMesh` picker with a **closest-*resolvable*-face-hit** selection rule (NOT closest geometric triangle). Möller–Trumbore in raw `[f32;3]` math; no glam dep added. Algorithm: iterate `world.query::<BRepHandle>()`, skip `brep_owner == None` candidates, collect all positive-t hits across every candidate's `ProjectedMesh.indices`, sort ascending by t, return the first hit that resolves to `Some(BRepFaceId)` via the existing `brep_face_id_for_triangle` query. Unlabeled / topology-changing / no-owner triangles are **transparent** to the picker — they do NOT mask resolvable faces behind them. The load-bearing punch-through integration test (`pick_punches_through_unresolvable_to_resolvable_behind`) demonstrates this with a Cuboid→Fillet front entity (unresolvable) and a plain Cuboid behind (resolvable): the picker returns the Cuboid hit at t=4.5, NOT None at the Fillet's earlier t. 6 unit tests in `picking::tests` for Möller–Trumbore correctness (dead-center / outside / parallel / behind-origin / glancing-edge / back-face) + 7 integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-projection/tests/face_picking_smoke.rs` (top-face baseline / nearest-along-ray / owner-missing → None / filleted-only → None / **punch-through (LOAD-BEARING)** / ray-misses-empty / bonus FaceSelection-composition via dev-dep). cad-projection production deps byte-identical (no editor-state production dep, no glam, no Cargo.toml dep changes whatsoever). The first GFX-side selection-substrate consumer of D-projection-α through γδ face-ID propagation; turns "user clicks → BRepFaceId → FaceSelection" from a pen-and-paper algorithm into a callable, tested primitive without assuming the renderer (no Camera modification, no GFX dep, no editor-shell window_event integration, no viewport widget, no UI feedback, no edge picking, no acceleration structure, no Fillet output identity answer — `FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md` STAYS PARKED, picker demonstrates the gap and does NOT close it). **The renderer/editor front half remains absent — picker is callable, not interactive; W21+ rendering wave will wire it.** +13 net workspace tests (was 2237; now **2250 tests**); 239 → 240 binaries (+1 for face_picking_smoke.rs); cad-projection 103 → 116 tests (+13 net = 6 picking unit + 7 face_picking_smoke integration); editor-state unchanged at 37; cad-core unchanged at 471. Derive `Ord` so `BTreeSet<FaceSelection>` iterates deterministically. **Phase 2 — `editor-state::FaceSelectionSet`**: BTreeSet-backed container with manual serde. Inherent methods: `new()` / `add` / `remove` / `contains` / `clear` / `len` / `is_empty` / `iter` (no traits). The pivotal method is `FaceSelectionSet::partition<F: Fn(&FaceSelection) -> bool>(&self, predicate: F) -> (Self, Self)` returning `(survivors, invalidated)`. **Caller-driven partition (decision D1)**; nothing automatically pruned; the projection state is data, the selection set is data, the caller composes them at decision points. **Phase 3 — editor-state Cargo.toml gains `rge-cad-core` dep** (for `BRepFaceId` + `BRepOwnerId` opaque ID type imports). `[forbidden-dep] PASS`: editor-state is Tier-2, cad-core is Tier-2; rule 3 only forbids cad-core from depending OUT, not inbound deps. `[editor-state-ownership] PASS`: lint forbids `cad_core` (without `rge_` prefix) but our import path is `rge_cad_core::...` so the leading-segment match doesn't fire; the editor-state ID-only-from-Tier-2 contract per PLAN §1.15 is satisfied because BRepFaceId + BRepOwnerId are opaque [u8; 16] ID types (not authoritative content — same role as EntityId in coordination state). **Phase 4 — `cad-projection::CadProjection::face_resolves_in_projection(entity, owner, face_id, world, graph) -> bool`**: owner-aware resolvability query; iterates the entity's projected mesh triangles via `brep_face_id_for_triangle`, returns `true` as soon as a triangle's resolved BRepFaceId matches `face_id`. Returns `false` on owner-mismatch (handle.brep_owner != Some(owner)) — including the legacy None-owner case — so a caller-driven partition uniformly classes mismatched/orphaned selections as invalidated. Lazy and per-call; nothing cached. **Layering preserved**: editor-state owns FaceSelection types + partition mechanic; cad-projection owns face_resolves_in_projection; neither crate depends on the other in production; caller composes via closure. cad-projection gains `rge-editor-state` ONLY as dev-dep (for the integration smoke). **Four load-bearing integration tests** in NEW `crates/cad-projection/tests/face_selection_partition_smoke.rs`: (1) `face_selection_partition_all_resolve_for_intact_cuboid` — substrate baseline. (2) `face_selection_partition_survives_cuboid_parameter_rebuild` — D-7.2-α owner-seeded contract lifted through cad-projection: capture 6 cuboid faces at 1×1×1, rebuild as 2×1×1, partition → ALL 6 in survivors. (3) `face_selection_partition_invalidates_side_selections_on_profile_count_change` — square Extrude → pentagon Extrude rebuild: 2 survivors (Bottom + Top, categorical caps per D-7.2-β) + 4 invalidated (square Side IDs disjoint from pentagon Side IDs since profile_count is in Side tag). (4) `face_selection_partition_invalidates_all_on_filleted_output` — **THE LOAD-BEARING PRESSURE TEST**: Cuboid → Fillet projection, FaceSelectionSet built from upstream cuboid's 6 face IDs, partition → ALL 6 invalidated (FilletOp emits unlabeled Tessellation AND resolver classifies Fillet as TopologyChangingOperator). The test docstring explicitly references `FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md`. The parked design note's "trigger 1: cad-projection integration" is now actively exercised in test code — but the design note STAYS PARKED. **Other 4 integration tests**: owner-mismatch invalidation; empty-set degenerate; unknown-entity invalidation; RON round-trip preserves partition outcome. **12 unit tests** in `editor-state::face_selection::tests`: round-trip serde (single + multi); partition with always-true / always-false / split / count-preserving predicates; deterministic iteration order; set scaffolding (add idempotent / remove returns presence / contains / clear / default empty). **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: cargo build 0 errors / 0 new warnings; editor-state 25 → 37 tests (+12 net = 12 face_selection unit); cad-projection 95 → 103 tests (+8 net = 8 integration); cad-core unchanged at 471 (no cad-core source modified); workspace 2211 → **2231 tests** (+20 net); nightly fmt --check exit 0 (after one mid-dispatch fmt apply); architecture-lints all PASS exit 0 — `[forbidden-dep] PASS (0 violations)` with the new editor-state→cad-core dep, `[editor-state-ownership] PASS (0 violations)` with the new `rge_cad_core::...` imports inside editor-state; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; rollout-debt count unchanged at 31. **HARD NON-GOALS observed**: no edge selections; no automatic pruning; no WorldSnapshot/PIE integration; no UI integration; no GFX picking; no Fillet output identity answer (FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md STAYS PARKED); no Selection (entity-only) modification; no BRepHandle / ProjectedMesh modification; no new substrate types beyond FaceSelection + FaceSelectionSet; no new traits (partition is inherent); no cad-projection→editor-state dep, no editor-state→cad-projection dep (both depend on cad-core for ID types only). **Public API delta**: (rge-editor-state) + `FaceSelection` + `FaceSelectionSet` + `FaceSelectionSet::partition` + lib.rs re-exports. | Phase 7 D-projection-γδ (cad-projection face-ID integration sub-γδ; Revolve mode-driven topology + Loft two-profile projection lookup) | **done 2026-05-09** — sub-γδ closes the cad-projection face-ID consumer matrix across all four direct providers. **Revolve `evaluate_full`**: switched `Tessellation::new` → `Tessellation::with_labels` with per-triangle `TopologyFaceId(edge_idx)` tags emitted in ring-major order (`2 * n * segments` total; each Side(i) appearing `2 * segments` times, interleaved across rings). **Revolve `evaluate_partial`**: side-wall triangles labeled identically to Full (ring-major Side tagging) followed by `n - 2` start-cap fan triangles all tagged `TopologyFaceId(n)` and `n - 2` end-cap fan triangles tagged `TopologyFaceId(n + 1)`. Both ops gained inline `debug_assert_eq!(face_labels.len(), indices.len() / 3)` invariants. **Consumer matrix CLOSED**: cad-projection now consumes `BRepFaceId` for Cuboid (sub-α) + Extrude (sub-β) + Revolve (sub-γ) + Loft (sub-δ) roots; all four direct providers emit face_labels through projection. | Phase 7 D-Fillet sub-δ (Add Loft support to FilletOp; input-side consumer contract closed) | **done 2026-05-09** — sub-δ closes the input-side consumer contract by adding the fourth direct-provider variant: `impl FilletUpstream for LoftOp` + `FilletOp::new_for_loft`. Loft has the same Bottom + Top + N Sides face structure and 3N clean 2-endpoint edges as Extrude (sub-β); the chamfer geometry adapts Extrude's face-normal-bisector approach to Loft's two-profile vertex layout (profile_a at bottom ring positions[0..N], profile_b at top ring positions[N..2N]). **Profile pairing convention (load-bearing)**: v0 inherits LoftOp's `profile_a[i]` ↔ `profile_b[i]` pairing exactly. **No twist matching, no rotation alignment, no coordinate-aware vertex correspondence is introduced by this dispatch**. If LoftOp ever extends to support twist or vertex correspondence, the chamfer geometry will need to be revisited; until then, the i-to-i convention is the substrate's contract. **Consumer matrix closure** — after sub-δ lands, FilletOp consumes BRepEdgeId from all four direct providers: Cuboid (sub-α, 12 of 12 edges chamferable; fixed topology); Extrude (sub-β, 3N of 3N edges chamferable; variable profile count); Revolve (sub-γ, 2N of 3N edges chamferable in Partial mode; 0 in Full mode; circular paths reject); Loft (sub-δ, 3N of 3N edges chamferable; two-profile, i-to-i pairing). The input-side consumer contract is now proven across the provider set. The next architectural conversation — output-side identity for FilletOp (impl BRepProvider / BRepEdgeProvider) — begins after this lands; it is NOT the next dispatch. **NEW `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet/loft.rs`** (~402L incl. 10 unit tests). All 3N Loft edges are chamferable in v0; no `UnsupportedEdgeGeometry` variant is ever returned for Loft inputs (mirrors Extrude). Bottom-perimeter edge i: bottom face normal (0, 0, -1) + profile_a's side normal at edge i; inward bisector = -(bottom + side)/2. Top-perimeter edge i: top face normal (0, 0, 1) + profile_b's side normal at edge i; inward bisector = -(top + side)/2. Vertical seam (Side(i) ∩ Side((i+1)%N)): average of four side-normal contributions across both profiles' adjacent edges; inward bisector = -(sum_of_four_normals)/4. Magnitude convention: half-bisector (~0.707) matching sub-α/β. Defensive `n_a.min(n_b)` pattern mirrors sub-7.2-ζ.δ's `BRepEdgeProvider` impl on LoftOp. **NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/loft_fillet_smoke.rs`** (9 integration tests). Four load-bearing sub-δ tests: (1) `fillet_loft_edge_ids_remain_valid_across_length_changes` proves rebuild-stability across length changes (length=1 edge ID valid against rebuilds at length=2 and length=0.5; FilletOp structural hashes byte-identical); (2) `fillet_loft_edge_ids_remain_valid_across_coordinate_changes_with_same_n` proves coordinate-only changes preserve edge IDs (substrate doesn't inspect coordinates per D-7.2-ζ.δ); (3) `fillet_loft_edge_ids_invalidated_by_profile_count_change` proves topology-change rejection across profile-count changes (LoftOp enforces equal counts so changing topology means changing both profiles together: sq×sq → pen×pen); (4) `fillet_loft_distinct_owners_produce_disjoint_specs` mirrors sub-α/β/γ owner-disjointness pattern. The 10 unit tests in `fillet/loft.rs::tests` cover validation (rejects zero/negative/non-finite radius + empty list + unknown edge ID), accept paths (single bottom-perimeter edge + all 3N edges), helper-table sanity (`loft_edge_vertex_pair_table_correctness` verifies for N=4: 0→(0,1), 4→(4,5), 8→(1,5)), and evaluation (one edge adds 2 verts + 2 tris; three edges linear growth). **Sub-α/β/γ tests preserved byte-identically**: all 7 sub-α `fillet_smoke.rs` integration tests + all 8 sub-β `extrude_fillet_smoke.rs` integration tests + all 9 sub-γ `revolve_fillet_smoke.rs` integration tests + all sub-α/β/γ unit tests pass byte-identically (sub-δ adds another `FilletUpstream` impl, not a public surface change). **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance — central success criterion): no twist matching / rotation alignment / coordinate-aware vertex correspondence (v0 inherits LoftOp's i-to-i profile pairing exactly); no real round-fillet kernel; no `impl BRepProvider for FilletOp`; no `impl BRepEdgeProvider for FilletOp`; no fifth operator support (after sub-δ the consumer pattern closes); no multi-edge corner-blending; no new substrate types (no `LoftFilletStrategy`, no `EdgeKindSelector`); no `FilletUpstream` trait modification (trait stays exactly as sub-γ defined it); no new public API surface (`FilletOp::new_for_loft` follows the precedent of `new_for_extrude` / `new_for_revolve`); no `Operator` / `OperatorNode` / `OperatorGraph` / `Tessellation` / `topo_lineage` / `cad-projection` / `gfx` / `kernel/*` modification; no `Cargo.toml` modification; no new ADR / lint / doctrine doc / §18 companion; no PLAN, IMPLEMENTATION, fileandfolderstructure, versions edits; no prior `fillet/` file modification beyond `mod loft;` in `mod.rs` (cuboid.rs / extrude.rs / revolve.rs byte-identical); no prior test files modified (`fillet_smoke.rs` / `extrude_fillet_smoke.rs` / `revolve_fillet_smoke.rs` byte-identical). | Phase 7 D-Fillet sub-γ (Add Revolve support to FilletOp + extract internal `FilletUpstream` trait; mode-driven topology consumer of BRepEdgeId) | **done 2026-05-09** — sub-γ generalizes the FilletOp consumer pattern to mode-driven topology (Revolve Full ↔ Partial). Internal architectural consolidation: extract a `pub(crate) trait FilletUpstream: BRepEdgeProvider` with one method `resolve_chamfer_spec(&self, canonical_index: usize) -> Result<ChamferSpec, &'static str>`. Extrude: all 3N edges supported (sub-β). Revolve Full: 0 edges supported — all side-side adjacencies are circular paths through `segments` vertices. Revolve Partial: 2N of 3N supported — cap-side adjacencies are clean 2-endpoint edges; side-side adjacencies are circular paths. | Phase 7 D-Fillet sub-α (Cuboid-only chamfer FilletOp; first BRepEdgeId consumer) | **done 2026-05-09** — sub-α ships `FilletOp` as the first real consumer of the `BRepEdgeId` substrate. | Phase 7 D-7.2-ζ.ζ (gate-closure stress test, 100 × 10 deterministic seeded) | **done** — NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/phase_7_2_gate_closure.rs` (~720L; 1 main gate test + 6 sanity tests on the harness machinery). Main gate test `phase_7_2_gate_closure_100_chains_10_rebuilds_seed_0x7e5a_dead_beef_c0de` builds 100 random chains via `generate_random_chain` (RootKind ∈ {Cuboid, Extrude, Revolve, Loft}, 0..=2 Transform wraps, regular polygons N ∈ {3, 4, 5, 6} for Extrude/Revolve/Loft, segments ∈ {3..=16} and angle ∈ (0, 2π] for Revolve), then for each chain applies 10 random mutations (preserving OR changing per a 50/50 coin flip on roots that support topology change; Cuboid roots only ever receive preserving mutations since Cuboid is fixed-topology). Each rebuilt chain resolves face+edge IDs through `brep_face_ids_for_node` + `brep_edge_ids_for_node` and the test asserts `assert_eq!` (preserving) or `assert_ne!` (changing) against the initial chain's IDs. Coverage gate `topology_preserving_count >= 100` and `topology_changing_count >= 50` ensures both branches are exercised; actual recorded counts on the fixed seed: **623 preserving + 377 changing = 1000 mutations**. Mutations target the root direct-provider's parameters (Transform-parameter mutations are always topology-preserving and would not exercise the "topology-changing" branch — sub-7.2-ε's smokes already cover those). Boolean / Sweep are not in the chain generator (the resolver returns `TopologyChangingOperator` for those — sub-7.2-ε's smokes cover those error paths). The 6 sanity tests (`tiny_rng_deterministic_for_fixed_seed`, `tiny_rng_rejects_zero_seed`, `chain_generator_visits_all_root_kinds`, `apply_preserving_mutation_keeps_topology_counts`, `apply_changing_mutation_alters_topology_counts_or_breaks_ids`, `cuboid_chain_only_uses_preserving_mutations`) exercise the harness on small fixed inputs to catch bugs before the full 1000-mutation gate. **No new substrate** — no new IDs, no new resolver functions, no operator changes, no `BRepProvider` / `BRepEdgeProvider` modifications, no enum extensions, no new traits. **No `Cargo.toml` modification** — hand-rolled xorshift64 `TinyRng` is the entire random infrastructure. **No prior test files modified** — all 9 prior B-Rep integration tests + 4 prior face-identity smokes + face_id directory + face_tag.rs + provider.rs + resolve.rs + edge_id.rs + edge_resolve.rs byte-identical. | Phase 7 D-7.2-ζ.ε (Graph-level B-Rep edge-identity resolver, Transform inheritance) | **done** — sub-7.2-ζ.ε ships **graph-level Transform inheritance for edges** via free `topology::edge_resolve::brep_edge_ids_for_node(graph, node, owner) -> Result<Vec<BRepEdgeId>, BRepResolveError>` over `OperatorGraph`; structural mirror of sub-7.2-ε's face resolver. | Phase 7 D-7.2-ζ.β/γ/δ (Extrude + Revolve + Loft B-Rep edge identity, compressed dispatch) | **done** — three additive `impl BRepEdgeProvider` blocks, one per direct face provider beyond Cuboid, all using `local_ordinal = 0`. **`ExtrudeOp`**: `3 * N` edges (N bottom-perimeter `Bottom ∩ Side(i)` + N top-perimeter `Top ∩ Side(i)` + N vertical-seam `Side(i) ∩ Side((i + 1) % N)` adjacencies). **`RevolveOp`**: `n` edges (Side-Side adjacencies only) in Full mode; `3n` edges (n axial seams + n start-cap-perimeter + n end-cap-perimeter) in Partial mode — driven by `is_full_revolution()` (the same canonical 1e-6-vs-2π discriminator the BRepProvider impl uses). **`LoftOp`**: `3 * N` edges (same shape as Extrude). Edge identity derives transitively from face identity — face-substrate's topology-change behavior (profile-count, segment-count, full-vs-partial mode) propagates through edge derivation by construction. **Compositional-honesty test covered explicitly**: `revolve_full_and_partial_edge_ids_are_disjoint` asserts mode break propagates to edge identity (Full = 4 edges, Partial = 12 edges, IDs disjoint). New unit tests inside the operators' existing `mod tests` blocks (3 per Extrude / 4 per Revolve / 3 per Loft = 10 unit tests). New integration smokes mirroring `cuboid_edge_identity_smoke.rs` precedent: `crates/cad-core/tests/{extrude,revolve,loft}_edge_identity_smoke.rs` (3+5+3 = 11 integration tests). **No `BRepProvider` / `BRepEdgeProvider` / `BRepEdgeId` modification** — sub-7.2-α/ζ.α substrate byte-identical. **No graph-level edge resolver** (sub-7.2-ζ.ε), **no `TopologyEdgeId`**, **no edge graph**, **no fillet prep**, **no fifth direct provider impl** — Boolean / Sweep / Transform stay un-tagged for both faces and edges. **No Cargo.toml edit / no new ADR / no new lint / no exemption added or removed**. | Phase 7 D-7.2-ζ.α (Minimum B-Rep edge-identity substrate, Cuboid only) | **done** — sub-7.2-ζ.α ships the **first slice of edge identity**: `BRepEdgeId` (16-byte BLAKE3-derived stable edge identity, derived from a sorted face pair plus a `local_ordinal: u32` slot), `BRepEdgeId::for_face_pair(face_a, face_b, local_ordinal)` constructor (sorts inputs lexicographically by `[u8; 16]` so order is irrelevant; domain separator `b"rge.cad.brep.edge/v1:"` distinct from face-id's `b"rge.cad.brep.face/v1:"`), and `BRepEdgeProvider` sibling trait (added alongside `BRepProvider` — NOT a supertrait extension, NOT a default-method extension, kept independent so partial rollout stays honest). `impl BRepEdgeProvider for CuboidOp` returns 12 edge IDs in canonical order (4 bottom-face perimeter, 4 top-face perimeter, 4 vertical) using a frozen 12-pair adjacency table; every edge has `local_ordinal = 0` (no two non-opposite cuboid faces share more than one edge). `local_ordinal` slot reserved for future operators with multi-edge face pairs (faces with holes, non-convex sweeps) — extends without v2 derivation-scheme migration. **Substrate-honest design**: face IDs are sorted before hashing so `for_face_pair(a, b, k) == for_face_pair(b, a, k)`; owner disjointness propagates transitively through face IDs (each `BRepFaceId` already includes owner in its derivation); domain separator prevents `BRepEdgeId` and `BRepFaceId` byte-collision even if their derivation inputs accidentally coincide. New module `crates/cad-core/src/topology/edge_id.rs` (226 lines incl. 9 unit tests covering determinism, order-independence, local-ordinal-distinguishes, distinct-pairs, owner-disjointness-via-face-ids, edge-id-distinct-from-face-id-via-domain-separator, byte-format round-trip, serde round-trip, Display format); `crates/cad-core/src/topology/provider.rs` extended with `BRepEdgeProvider` trait alongside the unchanged `BRepProvider`; `crates/cad-core/src/operators/cuboid.rs` adds the additive `impl BRepEdgeProvider for CuboidOp` block + 2 unit tests (`brep_edge_provider_returns_12_unique_edges`, `brep_edge_ids_align_with_canonical_adjacency_table`); new integration test file `crates/cad-core/tests/cuboid_edge_identity_smoke.rs` (2 integration tests: `cuboid_edge_ids_stable_across_parameter_rebuilds` mirroring sub-7.2-α precedent, `cuboid_edge_ids_distinct_across_owners`); `topology/mod.rs` adds `mod edge_id;` + `pub use edge_id::BRepEdgeId;` + extended `pub use provider::{BRepEdgeProvider, BRepProvider};`; `lib.rs` re-export list extended with `BRepEdgeId` + `BRepEdgeProvider` alphabetically. **Sub-7.2-ζ.α only — Extrude / Revolve / Loft `BRepEdgeProvider` impls, the graph-level edge resolver (Transform inheritance), `TopologyEdgeId` labels on `Tessellation`, edge graph, and Phase 7.2 IMPLEMENTATION.md exit criterion are subsequent dispatches.** No new ADR / no new lint / no new doctrine doc / no new §18 companion / no Cargo.toml edit / no exemption added or removed. WGSL emits `clip = camera.view_proj * vec4(position, 1.0)` + Lambert `max(dot(N, -L), 0)` + half-vector Phong specular against `view_dir = normalize(-world_pos)` (camera-at-origin assumption), output linear RGB so the SrgbU8 target encodes for free. **Pixel-level assertions PASS**: lit white quad center r/g/b > 200; backlit quad center r/g/b < 80 (ambient-only); 2x2 checker quad shows two distinct colors at left vs right halves. **Co-exists with existing 26-test substrate** — zero changes to `vertex.rs`/`mesh.rs`/`mesh_pipeline.rs`/`buffer.rs`/`transform.rs`/`context.rs`/`frame.rs`/`pipeline.rs`/`target.rs`. wgpu 29 quirks discovered: `Queue::write_texture` takes `TexelCopyTextureInfo` **by value** (not by ref); `SamplerDescriptor.mipmap_filter` is `MipmapFilterMode` (distinct type from `FilterMode`); `bytemuck::cast_slice(&[ubo])` creates a temporary that drops before `queue.write_buffer` reads it (E0716) → use `bytemuck::bytes_of(&ubo)` for single-struct uploads. |
| Phase 7.1 — `crates/cad-core` MVP D-prime | **done** — 33 new tests (32 unit + 1 integration smoke). 7 new modules under `crates/cad-core/src/`: `operators/{mod, cuboid, transform}.rs` (`Operator` trait + `OperatorNode` enum + `OpKind` + `EdgeKind::Input(port)`; `CuboidOp { width, height, depth }` arity 0 → 8-vertex/12-tri origin-centered box; `TransformOp { translation, rotation_quat_xyzw, scale }` arity 1 → applies `glam::Mat4::from_scale_rotation_translation` to upstream positions). `graph/operator_graph.rs` (`OperatorGraph` wraps `kernel/graph-foundation::Graph<OperatorNode, EdgeKind>`; content-derived NodeIds via BLAKE3; recursive `evaluate()` with cycle detection via in-flight ancestor `HashSet<NodeId>`; `effective_hash` recursively combines local + port + upstream so cache invalidates correctly when any upstream parameter changes). `checkpoints/mod.rs` (`CadGraph` wrapper owning `OperatorGraph` + `CheckpointHistory`; begin_operation / commit / rollback / restore_to; `MutationOutsideOperation` error guards `graph_mut()` access; `restore_to(C1)` test verifies state reverts from C2 with 3 nodes back to C1 with 1 node). `tessellation/{mod, mesh, cache}.rs` (`Tessellation { positions, indices }` with index-validity check; `Tolerance::new(t)` validates finite>0 and quantizes to `(t*1e9) as u64` for hash equality across float drift; `TessellationCache` HashMap keyed on `CacheKey { structural_hash: [u8; 32], tolerance }` with hit/miss tracking). | Phase 7 D-Extrude (first non-trivial cad-core operator) | **done** — 26 new tests (24 unit incl. 1 dispatch test in `operators/mod.rs`, 1 integration smoke in `tests/extrude_smoke.rs`). New `crates/cad-core/src/operators/extrude.rs` (670 lines): `Polygon2D` (closed CCW/CW-agnostic 2D polygon in XY plane; lazy convexity check via signed_area + adjacent-edge cross-product sign uniformity; ctor validates ≥3 finite points + no coincident adjacent points returning `Polygon2DError::{TooFewPoints, NonFiniteCoordinate, DegenerateEdge}`); `ExtrudeOp { profile: Polygon2D, length: f32 }` arity 0 (profile is parameter, not upstream input — same convention as `CuboidOp`); `evaluate()` validates `length > 0` and finite + profile.len() ≥ 3 + all points finite + `signed_area() != 0` + `convexity() == Some(true)` (concave rejected with `InvalidParameter` matching "convex"); CW input handled by reversing iteration order so algorithm always processes CCW; vertex generation: 2n vertices total (n bottom ring at z=0, n top ring at z=length); fan triangulation from vertex 0 for both caps with proper outward-facing winding (bottom face -Z normal, top face +Z); side walls as 2 triangles per ring edge; total triangle count = 4n-4 (2(n-2) cap tris + 2n side tris); 32-byte BLAKE3 structural_hash over (b"extrude:" || length || profile_len || profile_points). `OpKind::Extrude` + `OperatorNode::Extrude(ExtrudeOp)` variant added; `as_operator()` match arm extended; `lib.rs` re-exports extended (`ExtrudeOp`, `Polygon2D`, `Polygon2DError`). **Triangle (n=3) → 6 verts / 8 tris / 24 indices PASS; Square (n=4) → 8 / 12 / 36 PASS; Pentagon (n=5) → 10 / 16 / 48 PASS**. Integration smoke chains `CadGraph::begin_operation → add_operator(Extrude) → set_root → commit → evaluate` for a regular pentagon prism with length 2.5, asserting bottom z=0 + top z=2.5 + correct counts. **No external triangulation library** — fan triangulation suffices for convex profiles; concave support deferred to a separate dispatch with library scoping ADR (earcutr / lyon options). **Match-exhaustiveness audit**: zero downstream sites needed update — only `as_operator()` in cad-core itself pattern-matches `OperatorNode`; cad-projection only constructs variants. cad-core 33 → 59 tests. |
| Phase 7 D-Revolve (4th cad-core operator) | **done** — 19 new tests (17 unit incl. 1 dispatch test in `operators/mod.rs`, 1 integration smoke in `tests/revolve_smoke.rs`). New `crates/cad-core/src/operators/revolve.rs` (526 lines): `RevolveOp { profile: Polygon2D, segments: u32 }` arity 0; reuses `Polygon2D` substrate from D-Extrude; constructor validates `segments >= 3`; `evaluate()` validates profile.len() ≥ 3 + all points finite + all `x >= 0` (profile lies on +X side of Y-axis) + `signed_area() != 0`; **concave profiles ALLOWED** for full revolution (no fan-triangulated caps needed → no convexity restriction unlike Extrude); CW input handled by reversing iteration order. Algorithm: full 2π rotation around Y-axis with `segments` rotational steps; vertex generation `(x*cos θ, y, x*sin θ)` per profile point per ring; total `n*segments` vertices, `2*n*segments` triangles (no caps — full revolution closes on itself via index wrap `(s+1) % segments`). 32-byte BLAKE3 structural_hash over (b"revolve:" || segments || profile_len || profile_points). `OpKind::Revolve` + `OperatorNode::Revolve(RevolveOp)` variant added; `as_operator()` match arm extended; `lib.rs` re-exports extended (`RevolveOp`). **Critical correctness validations**: triangle profile (n=3) × 4 segments → 12 verts / 24 tris / 72 indices PASS; square (n=4) × 6 segments → 24 / 48 / 144 PASS; square × 8 segments via integration smoke → 32 / 64 / 192 PASS with every vertex r² ∈ {1, 4} confirming the inner/outer radii of the square cross-section + y ∈ [0,1]; concave L-shape profile accepted (no fan-triangulation difference from Extrude); axis-touching profile (vertex at origin) yields degenerate-but-valid mesh; CW profile auto-reversed; structural_hash deterministic + segments-sensitive + profile-sensitive; negative-x profile rejected with "x >= 0" InvalidParameter. **Side-wall outward radial winding verified** by explicit `revolve_first_quad_has_outward_radial_normal` unit test. **Match-exhaustiveness audit**: zero downstream sites needed update. cad-core 59 → 78 tests. **NOT in this dispatch**: partial revolution (angle < 2π) requires fan-triangulated caps (separate dispatch); arbitrary axis (use TransformOp upstream); helical sweep / loft (separate operators). |

Prior: D-7.2-δ Loft B-Rep face-identity substrate landed 2026-05-09 as the fourth `BRepProvider` impl, this time exercising the **two-input local-provider** topology axis: `LoftOp` is the first operator with two profile inputs, and the substrate handles this without leaking into chain-composition territory (sub-7.2-ε). Bounded additive dispatch in `crates/cad-core/src/topology/{face_tag,face_id,mod}.rs` + `crates/cad-core/src/operators/loft.rs` + new `crates/cad-core/tests/loft_face_identity_smoke.rs`: new `LoftFaceTag` 3-variant `#[non_exhaustive]` enum (`Bottom`, `Top`, `Side { edge_index: u32, profile_a_count: u32, profile_b_count: u32 }`) in canonical face-emission order matching `LoftOp::evaluate` (Bottom cap → Top cap → Side(0..N-1)); new constructor `BRepFaceId::for_loft_face(owner, tag)` mirroring extrude's scheme but with operator-kind separator `b"loft:"` + appended `edge_index.to_le_bytes() || profile_a_count.to_le_bytes() || profile_b_count.to_le_bytes()` for `Side` only (caps' BLAKE3 input ends after the discriminant byte); new `impl BRepProvider for LoftOp` returning `N + 2` pairs in canonical emission order. **Substrate-honesty design choice (load-bearing)**: `Side` carries BOTH `profile_a_count` AND `profile_b_count` independently — even though `LoftOp::evaluate` enforces equal counts at runtime (rejects `InvalidParameter` if `profile_a.len() != profile_b.len()`), the tag does NOT depend on that validation rule. Constructor handles unequal counts directly; `for_loft_face_handles_unequal_profile_counts_at_constructor_level` test verifies this. **A→B ordering is hashed**: swapping `profile_a` and `profile_b` produces different IDs for `Side(i)` (gate test `for_loft_face_distinct_for_swapped_profile_counts`). Stability contract pinned in `LoftFaceTag` docstring (7 clauses): caps stable across length AND coordinate-only profile changes (categorical, no inner data, matching ExtrudeFaceTag precedent); Sides stable across length and coordinate-only profile changes; Sides break when EITHER profile count changes; Sides depend on profile-A vs profile-B ordering; substrate does NOT inspect profile coordinates (rotation / twist matching / vertex-pairing offset OUT OF SCOPE for v0); no twist-matching implied (future twist param requires new variant or field). Defensive `n_a.min(n_b)` cap in `brep_face_ids` defends against hypothetical mid-mutation through the `pub profile_a` / `pub profile_b` fields without panic. `face_id.rs` reached 1078 lines (>1000) so a `// SPLIT-EXEMPTION:` annotation was added to its head documenting the cohesive owner-seed + per-operator face-identity constructor module that grows by ~12 tests + 1 constructor + 1 KIND const per per-operator BRepProvider sub-dispatch. Prior: D-7.2-γ Revolve B-Rep face-identity substrate landed 2026-05-09 as the third `BRepProvider` impl, this time exercising a topology axis no prior dispatch has touched: **categorical mode change** (Full vs Partial revolution alters the face *set itself*, not just the face count) plus segment-driven topology (segment count change breaks Side IDs by construction). Bounded additive dispatch in `crates/cad-core/src/topology/{face_tag,face_id,mod}.rs` + `crates/cad-core/src/operators/revolve/{mod,tests}.rs` + new `crates/cad-core/tests/revolve_face_identity_smoke.rs`: new `RevolveMode` 2-variant `#[non_exhaustive]` enum (`Full = 0`, `Partial = 1`) derived from `RevolveOp::is_full_revolution()` at the impl site (NOT a free parameter); new `RevolveFaceTag` 3-variant `#[non_exhaustive]` enum (`Side { side_index, profile_count, segment_count, mode } = 0`, `StartCap { profile_count } = 1`, `EndCap { profile_count } = 2`); new constructor `BRepFaceId::for_revolve_face(owner, tag)` mirroring extrude's scheme but with operator-kind separator `b"revolve:"` + appended `(side_index, profile_count, segment_count, mode_byte)` for `Side` variants and `profile_count` only for cap variants (caps' BLAKE3 input deliberately does NOT hash `segment_count` in — substrate honesty: caps don't over-encode); new `impl BRepProvider for RevolveOp` returning `n` pairs for Full mode and `n + 2` pairs for Partial mode in canonical emission order (sides first, then start cap, then end cap — matches `partial_path::evaluate_partial`). **Three substrate-honesty design choices (load-bearing)**: (1) Side carries `mode` byte → 359° → 360° crossing the full/partial boundary breaks Side IDs by construction; (2) Side carries `segment_count` → 8 → 16 segments break Side IDs by construction; (3) Caps carry `profile_count` ONLY → segment_count + angle changes preserve cap IDs (caps are fan-triangulations of the profile polygon; segment count is irrelevant to cap geometry). Gate tests cover all three: `for_revolve_face_distinct_across_modes`, `for_revolve_face_segments_change_breaks_side_id`, `for_revolve_face_caps_unaffected_by_segments` plus integration smokes. Stability contract pinned in `RevolveFaceTag` docstring: angle stable within Partial mode (45° → 90° → 135° preserves all face IDs); mode flip breaks Sides; segment-count change breaks Sides; profile-count change breaks Sides; caps stable across angle and segment_count within Partial; no caps in Full mode; substrate does NOT inspect profile coordinates (rotation-limit pin same as ExtrudeFaceTag — coordinate-aware identity is OUT OF SCOPE for v0). Workspace 1970 → **1990** (+20 net = 15 lib unit + 5 integration). cad-core lib 211 → 226; **289 / 289** cad-core tests pass. **`impl BRepProvider` count in cad-core after this dispatch: exactly 3 (Cuboid + Extrude + Revolve)**. **Sub-7.2-γ only — does NOT close Phase 7.2's IMPLEMENTATION.md exit criterion**; remaining sub-7.2-δ (Loft / fourth operator) / sub-7.2-ε (chain composition across `OperatorGraph`) / sub-7.2-ζ (edges + vertices) are subsequent dispatches. HARD NON-GOALS resisted: edges / vertices / fourth operator's `BRepProvider` impl / coordinate-aware rotation detection / raw-angle hashing / raw-geometry hashing / third `RevolveMode` variant / additional Side fields / `Operator` trait modification / `Tessellation` modification / `OperatorNode` / `OperatorGraph` modification / `Polygon2D` modification / `CuboidOp` / `ExtrudeOp` modification (prior impls byte-identical) / `provider.rs` modification / revolve geometry-test modification (only ADD test fns at bottom) / `cad-projection` / `gfx` / kernel integration / D-Fillet prep / new ADR / new lint / new doctrine / new §18 companion / Cargo.toml mods. Substantive architecture-lint exemptions remain at **0**; failure-class rollout-debt unchanged at **31**.

Prior: D-7.2-β Extrude B-Rep face-identity substrate landed 2026-05-09 as the second `BRepProvider` impl, this time with **variable topology** (a profile of `N` vertices yields `N + 2` faces). Bounded additive dispatch in `crates/cad-core/src/topology/{face_tag,face_id,mod}.rs` + `crates/cad-core/src/operators/extrude.rs` + new `crates/cad-core/tests/extrude_face_identity_smoke.rs`: new `ExtrudeFaceTag` 3-variant `#[non_exhaustive]` enum (`Bottom`, `Top`, `Side { edge_index: u32, profile_count: u32 }`) in canonical face-emission order matching `ExtrudeOp::evaluate` (Bottom cap → Top cap → Side(0..N-1)); new constructor `BRepFaceId::for_extrude_face(owner, tag)` mirroring the cuboid scheme but with operator-kind separator `b"extrude:"` + appended `edge_index.to_le_bytes() || profile_count.to_le_bytes()` for `Side` only (caps' BLAKE3 input ends after the discriminant byte); new `impl BRepProvider for ExtrudeOp` returning `N + 2` pairs `(TopologyFaceId(0), Bottom)`, `(TopologyFaceId(1), Top)`, `(TopologyFaceId(2 + i), Side { i, N })` for `i in 0..N`. **Substrate-honesty design choice (load-bearing)**: `Side` carries `profile_count` so topology changes (square N=4 → pentagon N=5) break face identity by construction — the BLAKE3 input bytes differ. Gate test `extrude_face_ids_break_when_profile_count_changes` asserts every `Side` ID across square and pentagon is disjoint while caps' IDs are EXPECTED to match (caps stable across both `length` AND `profile_count` per the v0 contract pinned in `ExtrudeFaceTag`'s docstring). Rotation-limit pin documented: profile-vertex-order rotation at the same count preserves `Side` IDs (substrate does NOT inspect profile coordinates) — coordinate-aware identity / rotation detection is out of scope for v0. Workspace 1956 → **1970** (+14 net = 11 lib unit + 3 integration). cad-core lib 200 → 211; 269 / 269 cad-core tests pass. **Sub-7.2-β only — does NOT close Phase 7.2's IMPLEMENTATION.md exit criterion**; remaining sub-7.2-γ (edges + vertices) / δ (chain composition across `OperatorGraph`) / ε (cad-projection integration) plus third-operator `BRepProvider` impls are subsequent dispatches. **~~Phase 6 §6.3 Gate B — editor idle-frame timing (hybrid)~~ DONE 2026-05-11.** New test-only harness `crates/editor-shell/tests/editor_frame_idle.rs` (48L) measures `EditorShell::tick_redraw()` against PLAN §13.2's ≤8 ms gate using **batch timing methodology** (N=1000 frames per batch × K=10 batches; P50/P95 across batch means) to clear the Windows `Instant` resolution floor (single-call ~100 ns is below `Instant` resolution; prior single-call harness halted on variance-30%-stop-if). Recorded (release-mode) **P50 = 0.000044 ms / P95 = 0.000047 ms / variance across batch means = 9.7%** — Gate B PASS by ~170 000× margin. **Test is `#[ignore]`-annotated** (release-only timing harness; debug build trips variance gate at ~39%); invoke via `cargo test -p rge-editor-shell --release --test editor_frame_idle -- --ignored --nocapture` — same pattern as the `#[ignore]d phase_3_memory_soak_one_hour` deferred bench mentioned in the 2026-05-11 bench-refresh entry. **Scope LOAD-BEARING**: this is the CURRENT empty-shell CPU-idle baseline (`EditorShell::new()` with no `cad_world`, no projection, no scene, no GPU, no winit event loop) — NOT a loaded-editor measurement. **Gate B status: CLOSED for current CPU-idle interpretation**, with explicit re-measure note: same harness shape re-runs against loaded shell once non-trivial editor systems / idle scene wire (future Phase 6 dispatch). BASELINE.md §13.2 appended with full row + scope-limitation note + harness pointer; IMPLEMENTATION.md Gate B line carries inline `**[CLOSED 2026-05-11 for CPU-idle interpretation: empty-shell P95 = 0.000047 ms; loaded re-measure deferred; see BASELINE.md §13.2]**` marker. Test-only dispatch (zero source / Cargo / gfx / kernel touches); **workspace test count: 2359 passed unchanged + 17 → 18 ignored** (+1 discoverable test). Gates A (60fps simple-scene) and C (render-thread stable snapshot) remain deferred — A needs methodology ADR + scene authoring; C blocks on the sim/render thread split (PLAN §1.5.2).

~~Recommendation post-§18-docs-pack-6 superseded by deep-audit findings~~ — see post-deep-audit recommendation above.

Phase 6 §6.3 exit criteria status: ~~60fps on simple-scene golden project (1k cubes + 1 directional light)~~ **[Gate A CLOSED 2026-05-11 on recorder host only: NVIDIA RTX 4060 Ti / Vulkan / 1280×720 / static camera / min-of-3 P95 = 0.112 ms; NOT universal/vendor/thermal/cold-start/CI; see BASELINE.md §6.3]**; ~~editor frame ≤ 8ms idle~~ **[Gate B CLOSED 2026-05-11 for CPU-idle interpretation; loaded re-measure pending]**; ~~render-thread sees stable snapshot~~ **[Gate C CLOSED 2026-05-11 for ADR-117 RenderHandoff boundary invariant: single-threaded proxy today; future dedicated renderer thread must keep the same invariant; does not certify a full render-thread architecture yet; see `render_input_boundary.rs::gate_c_held_snapshot_stable_across_subsequent_publishes` + ADR-117]**; ~~100 material instances share one PSO~~ **[CLOSED 2026-05-11 via commit 54cec89; see §6.3 PSO-sharing gate in `gfx::tests::material_intent_pso_sharing`]**. Abort: render-snapshot overhead >5% of frame budget.

**Reconciled 2026-05-21 against [`plans/IMPLEMENTATION.md`](plans/IMPLEMENTATION.md) — the authoritative phased plan.** The v0 critical path is closed: Phases 0.2 / 1 / 2 / 4 / 5 / 7.1 / 7.2 / 7.3 / 7.4 exit criteria all met. **Phase 3** (WASM hot-reload — the constitutional bet) closed all four formal gates 2026-05-11, re-validated 2026-05-12: hot-reload p95 < 100 ms, ECS-via-WASM ≤ 1.5×, 1-hour soak, 100-cycle preservation. **Phase 7** (the CAD moat) closed 7.1 / 7.2 / 7.3 / 7.4 — 7.2 persistent topology IDs CLOSED 2026-05-09 (commit `ae31dee`), 7.3 cad-projection minimal CLOSED 2026-05-11 (`phase_7_3_gate_closure.rs`). Phase 6.1 + 6.2 + 6.3 done including the frame-graph substrate (umbrella close-out 2026-05-12). **v0 was release-certified 2026-05-14.** **Phase 8 (graph-foundation) CLOSED 2026-05-21** via batch sweep #65–#84: (1) **4 graph types share substrate primitives** — `OperatorGraph` (cad-core) / `MaterialGraph` / `AnimGraph` / `ScriptGraph`, spec asked for 3; (2) **cross-graph diff** validated in `crates/editor-ui/tests/phase8_graph_diff_smoke.rs` + full GraphDiff coverage matrix (edge-mut / node-mut / endpoint-change / removed-edge-record / added-edge-record / removed-node-payload / added-node-payload / ScriptGraph wrapper); (3) **editor `node_graph` widget renders all 4** via shared `&dyn VizAdapter` (`crates/editor-ui/src/widgets/node_graph.rs` + 5 smoke files including the combined `node_graph_phase8_three_domain_smoke.rs`); (4) **graph-foundation ADR governance held** — ADR-115 + amendment, ADR-097 backfilled (#78). Phase 8 abort condition (primitives too narrow / too broad) did NOT fire. No open §3.x / §7.x / §8 exit-criteria gap remains. The real next frontier is **Phase 9 (production pressure)** per IMPLEMENTATION.md §9 — eight evaluation axes (§0.6 freeze validity, abstraction pain, invalidation economics, reflection scale, async orchestration, compile times, editor usability, GPU pressure) — plus the carry-over kernel cavities (`shared`, `asset-streaming`, `io-scheduler`, `job-system`, `asset-view`), which should fill only under real consumer pressure.
